1b1(kha skong): zla shA du/rdza/ /b+hU /tu du/
1b2(kha skong): 'jigs byed kyi rtog pa'i rgyud kyi rgyu ba po/dag gi dbang phyug la phyag 'tshal lo//de nas
1b3(kha skong): 'dir ni bshad bya ba//ji ltar 'phro rnams zad/byed pa//sdug bsngal rnams mthar byed pa yi//
1b4(kha skong): bsgrub bya'i thabs chen mchog gyur pa//gsang/sngags de las 'byung bar 'gyur//dang po rnam
2a1(kha skong): dang 'gyu ba //myunodang mtha' ma gnyis /ldan g+ha/mchod rten sreg byed mtha' dang bcas/kha
2a2(kha skong): du shes par mi 'gyur ro//rdo rje can gyi mtha' lag naskye//yi ge 'dum khrig khri brjod na//nyams pa thams/
2a3(kha skong): cing sel bye cing //zhi dang rgyas dang dbang mngon spyod//sod dang spyod dgug dbye rongs dang //dman par byed dang
2a4(kha skong): rgyal srid sogs//thob pa nyid la the tshom med//dur khrodang tshi ba blod ngogs rtsub//shing gcig khang stong mtshan cig
2a5(kha skong): dpe ma khang 'dod gnas su bsam gtan brtsam//de nas bcom ldan 'das chos thams cad la byed pa me long
2b1(kha skong): lta bu zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/sku dang ye shes thams cad la khyab par bya ba'i phyir/sku mdog dkar po zhal draH/
2b2(kha skong): dang ldan par byas nas/'jig rten pa thams cad la gzigs nas/rang gi rigs kyi yi ge nyid brjod pas sku dang gsung dang
2b3(kha skong): thugs dang yon tan dang phrin las dang ye shes kyang gcig gi ngo bo sprul pa'i skur gyur to//kye ma bcom ldan rdo rje che//don rnams
2b4(kha skong): bskyed pa yang nyid do//mkha' dkyil 'od kyis 'gengs 'gyur ba//slar zhing kha dog lnga ldan pa//sa bon sngags kyis bskul ba
2b5(kha skong): yi//'od kyi rtse phran thub pa'i sku//kun kyang sangs rgyas gnas las skyes//rang la zhugs pas sku rdzogs gyur//zhal drug khro gnyer
2b6(kha skong): rab brjid pa//me he'i zhal lnga ni steng gnas pa//'jam dpal zhal ni 'dzum bcas bzhugs//lhag ma dkar dang ser dang
3a1(kha skong): dmar//du ba'i mdog mtshungs gyen skar ldan//thod pas ma rlon rgyu ma sprul//rus pa rdo rje phreng bas brgyan//glang chan rtag
3a2(kha skong): lpags gyon nas ni//hUM phaT glur len gad mo can//nam mkha'i lus can khro bo'i sprin//yang dang yang du spro byed pa'i//phyag /drug rab tu brjid
3a3(kha skong): pa yi//dbyug pa tho ba gtun shing dag/g.yas pa'i phyag gis rim bzhin 'dzin//dpra sta dang ni lcags kyu dang //zhags pa g.yon pa'i
3a4(kha skong): phyag gis 'dzin//pad+ma nyi ma ma he dang //gshin rje'i steng na 'gying dag can//zhabs drug g.yon kyang gar gyi gnas//'jig rten bdag po mthar mdzad pa'o//
3a5(kha skong): de ltar gang zhig dad pa dang //blo ldan g.yo sgyu rab spangs shing //legs par dbang rnams thob byas nas//rdo rje slob dpon mnyes byed pas//
3a6(kha skong): yang nas yang du dran byed na//brtan pa chen po thob par 'gyur//lha yi dge 'dun la nyon//dang po chang la rab dga' zhing //sha chen
3b1(kha skong): rtag tu mur byed na//las rnams de yis myur du 'grub//sku ni du ma 'phro byed cing //sku la sku rnams nges thim byed//thams cad sgyu ma nyid shes pas//'jig rten rnams su yang sad byed//khong stong kha dog
3b2(kha skong): dkar ba ste//rgyun tu rlung ni 'dzag par byed//chu skyes dmar po kha sbyar gnyis//yan lag gnyis kyis legs par bcun//shes pa 'phel ba me dang rlung //nyi ma zla ba thabs ldan dang //shes rab ldan par shes par
3b3(kha skong): bya//gnyis po de nyid rnam spangs na//khong du chud par mi 'gyur ro//chu skyes kha sbyor la brten te//gsum gnas pa yi ting 'dzin la//rdo rje chos kyis btab pa yis//thabs dang shes rab grol ba'i rgyun blo ldan
3b4(kha skong): 'das pa shes par 'gyur//de phyir de la brtson par bya//chos rnams chos nyid dbyer med pas//stong pa nyid kyi ye shes che//mi shigs rtog bral mtshan ma med//bde chen ye shes rdo rje sku//ye shes mi
3b5(kha skong): rtog rtog pa bral//rtog pa'i mtshan ma thams cad sreg/spros pa'i mtshan ma mtha' dag ni//ji snyed sgyu ma'i rnam par shes//de nyid shes nas grol ba'o//ma shes pas ni phyir zhing 'khor//'jig rten
3b6(kha skong): skye bo blo ldan 'gas//nges par rtogs pa thabs kyi mchog/sdug bsngal chen pos rab 'jigs nas//bde ba 'dod pas nan tan bya//dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rtog pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po las/thabs dang shes rab kyi
3b7(kha skong): bsam gtan bstan pa'i le'u ste dang po'o////de nas yang dag bshad bya ba//sngags p+ta las byung ba yi//las rnams 'dir ni shes bya ste//der ni lha yi sku yang
4a1(kha skong): sgyur//zhe sogs bzlas pa'i rim pa la//rdo rje'i dbus su rdo rje ni// zla la brten yi go yi//phreng ba kha dog lngar shes pa//skyen bul spangs nas klag pa na//mkhas pa
4a2(kha skong): bzlas pa'i rim pa'o//drag po'i las rnams sgrub pa la//nyon mongs bcod pa'i 'khor lo ni//sngon po rtse rtsibs bcu pa la//'od zer sna tshogs 'phro ba bsam//zhi bar 'dod pa'i skyes bu des/
4a3(kha skong): sems ni yang dag mnyam bzhag nas//sngags kyi 'od kyang 'gro gzhan la//phan pa'i yid dang ldan par bya//grog ras dang shing shun la//gur kum gi zhe dri rnams kyis//mchod rten rim pa lnga ldan
4a4(kha skong): ning /gdugs dang 'khor lo ldan par bya//sgrub pa po yi ming dang rus//de yi bum pa'i nang du bri//rten 'brel snying po la sogs pa'i//sngags kyis g.yon nas bskor ba bre//cig shos g.yas nas
4a5(kha skong): yon du bri//de la spel tshig med pa 'am//yang na 'khor lo'i bar du bzhag/'khor lo kun la kha sbyor gnad//rab tu gnas par byas nas kyang //lus sam mgul lam gang bder bzhag/des
4a6(kha skong): gdon dang byed snyems dang //rims dang yams rnams sel bar byed//gang zhig yul rnams gzhom 'dod na//hU~M gi sa bon dang ldan par//ming yig tsam po bri bar bya//so phrag phye ma ldeng ros
4a7(kha skong): dang /ba bla ma he'o khrag gis brdzis//zla gam gnyis pa'i gzugs byas te//brar du gang 'dod bsgrub pa yi//gzugs brnyan sor brgyad pa yi tshad//byas la gan rkyal du bzhag la//ma he gdong yi
4b1(kha skong): sbyor ba yis//khri phyag gcig tu sngags bzlas nas//dum bu dum bur gtubs byas te//chu bo'i gzhung du gtor byas na//skad cig de la de dbang 'gyur//bya rog 'ug pa'i gzugs byas te//ma nu mA li ro tsa nas//khyo
4b2(kha skong): shugs bsgrub bye'i ming bris te/gshin rje'i phyogs bltas gisang sngags gdon//rkang pa g.yon pas mnan nas ni//mi yi rje ngar phur bus gdab//skad cig tsam la de dag dbye//de nas 'dir ni bsad pa yi//
4b3(kha skong): cho ga'i rim pa bshad par bya//zhal drug phyag drug zhabs drug pa 'am//yang na zhal bzhi phyag bzhi pa'am//zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa yang rung //ma he gdong pa'i sbyor ba yis//khrag rnams sna tshogs tha
4b4(kha skong): dang dang //bsrub bya'i rjes dang dug gi rigs//rta dang ma he bung bu'i chus//smras pa'i bsgrub bya'i ling ga bya//lus la tsher mas gzugs bya zhing //til mar gyis kyang bslu bar bya//yang na shring lo gr-i ga'am//
4b5(kha skong): dur khrod ras som shun pa la//rang nyid gcer bu skye bshig nas//lus ni thal bas byu gros byas ste//mngon sum khros nas sha chen bza'//rab tu zhim pa'i charab tu zhi /nag po'i chos kyi mtshan phyed dus/
4b6(kha skong): 'khor lo bri bar brtsam par bya/ling tshi bcu gnyis 'khor lo ni//hUM dang hrIHSh+T+rIHdbus su dgod//Na yai ne ra rtsibs mtshan la//yungs kar ti la dang skar chu dang //rta dang ma hA khyi dag khrag/bya rog 'gyu ba'i sgra
4b7(kha skong): yis bre//yi ge ya yi lto bar yang //ming dang rus su ldan pa bris//phyogs bzhir yi ge bcu pa ni//ming dang bcas pa bri bar bya//brgyad po dag la rol pa bzhin//yi ge 'di dge bri'ir bya//mo ya man+ta
5a1(kha skong): dza kU la ru pa a mu ka kA ra ya hUM hUM phaT phaT swA hA//yi ge rnams la bskor nas ni//bsgrub bya gzug dang ldan pa bli//da yi mu khyud dka la ni//yi ge bcu pa ming bcas pro//
5a2(kha skong): phyogs bzhir rtse gsum rdo rjes mtshan//de bzhin rjes rnams ma lus pas//'khor lo lte bar ldan pa bri//gshin rje'i gzugs ni ral gri dang //dbyig pa 'dzin pa bris nas ni//de dang de nyid lto sbyang la//
5a3(kha skong): mtshan ngan thod pa'i nang du gzhug/tsha ga snyam ske tshe dug ma zi//ro \u0f85sa bkang nas dkyil 'khor ni//gru gsum dbus su bzhag par bya//yungs dang bra ngos lu nag/dza b+hi bra bo sogs rnams la//gsang
5a4(kha skong): sngags rgyal po brjod byas te//dro'am du baM 'thul bar du//rim dang rim gyis khrag rnams ni//ma lus zad par 'thung ba ye//ma yengs par ni bsam gtan bya//yang na bsgrub bya za bar mthong //
5a5(kha skong): shing gcig car ni rengs pa dang //mal 'og tu ni zhwa zhing lkugs//chu mdor byed cing ri rtse bskrad//bsad pa me thab 'og tu sba//dgug pa la ni sgo khang 'og/lha 'am 'khor li sbyar ba'o//bde gnas
5a6(kha skong): rnams kyis dbang du 'gyur//mar khu chen po thod pa yi//nang du blugs nas bskol byas te//bzhir byas mig la byug byed na//mngon shes de nyid myur du 'thob//rigs ldan rgyal po las rnyed cing //mdog
5a7(kha skong): ldan lang tshogasang bkug la//tsan dar lde gu rang byas te//las kyi sbyor bas de nyid bcing //yang na me la gdung bas dru //oM pradz+ra kro tA ya marA dzaH/badz+rI kI li kI la ha na ha na mA ra ya phaT/ces bya'o//
5b1(kha skong): gsang sngags brjod byas la//rus pa'o phud pa gdab par bya//gsal shing la btsugs snrebA ya//rdzas la brnyan to bskru par bya//til ma thugs la rjod pas bzhar//mang me byas pa'i dud pa las//ma gnon dan na
5b2(kha skong): 'grub par 'gyur//gsang sngags rgyal po thogs med la//bsten pas thob bya mang yod kyang //'di ni brjod pa ci zhig dgos//yang na 'di ltar shes bya ste//rang nyid sngags dang ting 'dzin ldan//brtson chen gzhan du ma
5b3(kha skong): /yengs pas//gang du brtsams pa ni 'grub 'gyur//smad 'tshong rang byung nyid kyis ni//sngon bstan tsakra legs bris te//ling ga'i snying khar bcug byas la//rang mdun khrag gi zla gam ste//khrag gis byugs pa'i steng
5b4(kha skong): du bzhag/mi 'am rgyal po'i bu mo dag/dgug dang dbang gi yi grwa yis//de nyid du ni nges par 'gyur//nyal ba'i 'og tu mnan par bya//mi glang ra khyi bo phag khrag/'khor lo dris nas ling ga yi//mgrin dang
5b5(kha skong): bcu ga nas bya rog gi/khrag gis khrag skyug sngags bris nas//yi ge de ldan thod pa ru//bcug nas gsang sngags mang bzlas te//dur khrod me thab 'og bzhag na//khrag skyug pa la the tshom med//bsros na che ba'i
5b6(kha skong): nad kyi 'chi//sbal khrag pa wang klad pa yis//'khor lo de nyid legs bris nas//ling ga'i mchan khung g.yon bcug la//g.yas g.yon sbrul khrag glang khrag byugs//ling ga'i phyogs su rang nyid kyi/
5b7(kha skong): nga ba galar ba'i mthe bos mnan//de tshe bzlas pa mang byas nas//rgya gram lam du mnan la bzhag/de nas bzlog pa bris nas ni//shing gcig khong par sbas na rengs//rnga mo bya rog rgan po'i khrag/'khor
6a1(kha skong): bris nas ling gA yi//rkang gnyis par bcug rang mdun du//khrag gis rnga mod gzugs bris te//de yi steng bzhag rang nyid kyis//rlung gi bsam gtan ngos ldan na//bskrad pa nyid du rje
6a2(kha skong): chom med//ri bo dz+wa la 'dzegs te swa//ne'u le sbrul rta ma he dang //bya rog 'ug pa'i khrag gis ni//khyo shug rkang po'i rjes skyes pa'i//ling gsor brgyad par byas te//khral/des bris pa'i 'khor lo dag/snying
6a3(kha skong): khar bcug pa gnyis byas te//ne'u le gzugs byas steng du bzhag/lag gnyis rta dang ma he yi//rus pas brdung zhing gsang sngags zlos//rtse drung shing khar sbas na 'byed//tsan+da dkar pos legs bris
6a4(kha skong): nas/'gasar sogs rin chen rdzas su dril//mdun du zla ba'i gzugs steng du//bzhag pa nyin re bskor ba ni//ji srid byas nas bsrung bar nges//spyi bor btags na g.yul las rgyal//rkang par btag sma na
6a5(kha skong): chu steng 'gro//ba yi 'o mas khyas byas te//ku shu ba mar sogs mchod nas//gsol btab nad rnams thams cad bsrung //de nas bcom ldan 'das las phra ba thams cad las rgyal ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin
6a6(kha skong): lo snyoms par zhugs nas//las thams cad kyi rjes su 'gro ba'i sngags 'di/sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo //m+bA ra ya phaT/ces pa bsad pa'i 'o//bi dwe Sha ya dbye ba'i 'o//ut+pA Te ya bskrad
6a7(kha skong): ba'i'o//mo ha ya tshangs pa'i'o//wa shaM ku ru dbang du bya ba'i'o//swA s+thA ya mnan pa'i'o/ar+tha kaR+Sha ya dzaHdgug pa'i'o//oM hrIHswA hA/kha dang lag pa bshal ba'i sngags so//oM hrIHSh+T+rI
6b1(kha skong): kr-i tA nA nahUM sarba sha trUnan+t+ra shA ya stAm+b+ha ya phaT phaT swAhA/skyung po'i sngags so//oM hrIHk+Sha la R+ShA ba g+h+ra ba/nye ba'i snying po'o//oMhrIHkruM nr-i s+yo dz+yo hU~M la/snying po dam pa'o//oM Sh+T+rIHhUMHD+hom+bAt+ma kra d+ha gats+tsha drAN+Da
6b2(kha skong): smat+sa dzA pra ti gr-ih+Na pra sA di de bi ShAM ku ru swA hAM/spyan drangs pa'o//oM hIHSh+TiHhaHyon chab b+h+yo//oM hU~M hUM paT zhabs bsil lo//oM sarba duSh+Ta satwa da ma ka ga ga/ces pa dri chab kyi sngags so//oM ku mA rA ru pa Ni dzaMH
6b3(kha skong): /dzaHhUM phaT/me tog 'bul ba'i sngags so//oM hrIHhaHhe phaT/bdug pa'i'o//oM kA la rU pa sarba duSh+Ta satwa da ma kaM ma hA b+hU ta pa ti i maM ba ling gr-ih+Na gr-ih+NA pa ya swA hA//gtor ma'i sngags so//oM dIp+ta lo tsa
6b4(kha skong): /na be kr-i tA na na mahA nA nA hA sa nA dI naM dIp+ta ya swA hA//mar me'i sngags so//o dza ya dza ya su dza ya bi shwaR+ShA pa d+hi ri gats+tsha gats+tsha swas+thA ni kr-i taM ta na ta thA ga tash+tsa bi sardza ya ma ma kA n+yaM ku ru swA hA/ces pa gsheg su gsol ba'o//
6b5(kha skong): sngag so//de nas rdo rje 'dzin pa nyid//chos thams cad kyi rjes su 'gro ba dang //ldog pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/gsang sngags yongs su rdzogs pa'i 'phrin las 'di nyid bka' stsal to//
6b6(kha skong): nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par//hUM las yongs su rdzogs pa yi//rdo rje 'jigs byed bsam par bya//dmar po zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa//srin po rab tu khros pa 'dra//dbyug pa thod khrag phyag na
6b7(kha skong): na//ma he pad+ma nyi ma la//g.yon brkyang ba yi tshul gyi sdom//i ya man+ta kr-ita hUM phaT/gsang sngags rgyal po 'di bzlas na//'dod pa'i dngos grub thams cad 'byung //nam mkha'i dbyings su dbus
7a1(kha skong): mnas pa//sa chos sngon noms skyes pa'o// mas smya ni// sgyu ma/smyo gyu nga gos sa //blo la brjo pa/
7a2(kha skong): dang //dgra p+ta dang ni thong khrab dang //phyag bzhi po na rim pas 'dzin//ma he nag po'i zha pa stong ni//'jam dpa' zhag ni ser zhing 'jug/dpa' bo chen po rang nyid na mo/rab tu
7a3(kha skong): zhim pa'i chang btung zhing //sha chen dang kyang myur ba bya//mtshan modur khrod byed cing //rtag par phasang sngags bzlas par bya//thig le 'dren pa'i rnal 'byor ni//bsgrub bya'i phyogs su bsam
7a4(kha skong): pabar bya//las rnams myur du 'dis 'grub po//yang na 'di lta shes bya ste//ma he ladong gi sbyor ba yis//sku yi kho 'og sngo sor shes//khyad par du ni bsad pa la//nag po ma he'i
7a5(kha skong): zhal can ni//rtse gsum lcags kyu 'dzin pa ste//ma he sha steng ba ma byas na//khrag 'dron pa yi mchog tu gsungs//res 'ga' khru la khro ba'o//lcags kyu 'dzin pa grangs med
7a6(kha skong): spro/zla ba spyang sus zin dus su//byi la'i sder me ra rnying dang //bya yi khris dang mi rus bsre//gang la phol pa skyo bar 'gyur//dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rtog de'i rgyud kyi rgyal po
7a7(kha skong): las sbyor ba'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o////de nas yang ngas bshad bya ba//sgrub par byed pa'i rnal 'byor pas//dur khrod ras sam dpa' bo gos//yang na
7b1(kha skong): dang 'byung ba //ma rgod mtha' ma gnyisaldan g+ha/mchod rten sreg byed mtha' dang bcas//gan
7b2(kha skong): du shes par mi 'gyur ro//rdo rje can gyi mtha' lag naso//yi ge 'bum khrig khri brjod na//nyams pa thams

8a1(kha skong): mkha' la khyer//rkang du ma khrag dum ro langs dang //wa dang sbyang ki gtum po dang //mkha' gro bo mo sha zla'i tshogs//bya dang gcan gzan sna tshogs bri//spyi bung \u0f7f/
8a2(kha skong): tu 'jigs bris nas//dar ni sgrub pa po yang bri//gri thod bzung nas sha chen mur//gos nag gyon nas khrag chen 'thung //rta dang ma he rus pa yi//phreng ba bzung nas gsang sngags 'don//
8a3(kha skong): bcom ldan 'das la blta ba bri//de ltar bris nas chang dang khrog/sha tshon go ro tsa nas mchod//mnyam gzhag g+ha yi dge 'dun des//dus gsu ma rgyun tu mchod byed na//rdo rje 'dzin pa myur du
8a4(kha skong): thob//sku ni rab tu sba zhing gsang //phan yon dam pa 'di las 'byung //dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rtog pa'i rgyal po las/bris sku'i le'u ste gsum pa'o///
8a5(kha skong): de nas yang dag bshad par bya//rtog pa ma lu saM zad byed cing //las rnams thams cad 'grub 'dod pas//blo ldan ser sna rnam spangs te//brtul phad g.yeng ba rnam spangs nas//sbyin sreg
8a6(kha skong): las la rab brtson bya//mtshal dang pa bla ldong ros dang //bshan pa'i go thal dur khrod sa//mi dang ma he khrag kis brdzi//khru do ba la khyu phyed rtsig/gru bzhi'i steng du zlum po ni//rdo rje rgya gram ldan
8a7(kha skong): byas la//de steng 'khor lo rtsibs dubye la//mtshan ma god par bya//lte bair me yi dkyil 'khor ni//mtho gang ched du byas pa la//ma he'i khrag gis legs par byug/bdag nyid lho
8b1(kha skong): phyogs bltas te//ma he zhal gyi sbyor ba yis//thob kyi nang gi lci ba la//me yi sa bon mngon paltas la//bskal pa'i de chen lta bur sgom//dar ni me lha bsgom bya ste//zhal gsum phyag drug nag
8b2(kha skong): drub//phyag gnyis 'ang 'dra'i yu mo la 'khyud//g.yas pa'i phyag gis 'gro rnams la//skyabs sbyin mdzad cing bgrang phreng 'dzin//g.yon pas ril ba mchog stsol brtson//zhabs drug rigs drug
8b3(kha skong): mtshon ma brjes//zhal nas me rnams rab 'phro zhing //'od rnams sna tshogs rnams kyis brgyan//de ltar shes nas rab bsregs na//'dod pa'i don rnams rab tu 'byung //dgra bo'i gzugs rnams sha
8b4(kha skong): chen dang //chang dang ma he'i khrag bcas pa//stong phrag gsum du bsregs byas na//bsgrub bya khrag tu sgyu gas nas 'chi//glang po rta bo khyi sha la//stong phrag gsum gyis dbang du byed//bya rog 'ug pa
8b5(kha skong): khyi sha chu//bsregs na me lha 'bye bar 'gyur//til dang nas dang pr-i sA lu//yung ba gi wi so phag rnams//stong phrag drug tu gang bsregs pa//longs spyod thams cad rnyed par 'gyur//rta dang rnga
8b6(kha skong): mo bya rog sha/mi sha rdo rje chur bcas pa//gsang sngags rnal 'byor ldan byas te//'argya rtsa brgyad kyis nges par skrod//ra sha daN+Da ut+pa ba//chang dang ma he chur bcas pa//gang 'dod brgya rtsa brgyad
8b7(kha skong): kyis thugs//dug dang khrag dang sgog pa dang //sha chen til mar rab spags te//brgya rtsa brgyad du bsregs byas na//pha rol gzhan gyi gsung sngags gcod//tsan+da dkar po 'bras dkar dang /

10a1(kha skong): sbyor bas ni//gsang sngags rgyal pos 'dod pa rgyur//ma yongs rje gcig sems kyis bya//gsungs dang ma gsungs mtha' dag kyang //ji lta ba yi rim pa yis/
